<script>
      var googletag = googletag || {};
      googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

          googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
      });

          pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
          pbjs.enableAnalytics([{
                provider: 'pubwise',
                options: {
                    site: 'd2a5ef67-8fed-4d00-9918-927ea7374a10',
                    endpoint:'https://api.pubwise.io/api/v4/event/add/'
                    }
                }]
          );
          pbjs.requestBids({
              bidsBackHandler: sendAdserverRequest
          });
      });

      function sendAdserverRequest() {
          if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
          pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
          googletag.cmd.push(function () {
              pbjs.que.push(function () {
                  pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                  googletag.pubads().refresh();
              });
          });
      }

      setTimeout(function () {
          sendAdserverRequest();
      }, PREBID_TIMEOUT);

</script>

        <div class="player-info-box-pos">OF</div></div>

                        </div>
                    </td>

                    
                    <tr><td><hr class="player-page-info-sep"/><div class="player-page-rotowire"><strong><a href="https://www.rotowire.com/users/ad_jump.asp?id=688&playerid=13128">RotoWire News</a>:</strong> Tucker went 1-for-3 with two RBI in Monday's Grapefruit League game against the Blue Jays. (3/20/2018)</div></td></tr>

                <tr><td><hr class="player-page-info-sep"/><table class="player-page-news"><tr>
                    <td>4/20/2016</td><td class="td-badge"><div class="rg badge">RG</div></td><td><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/deep-league-waiver-wire-hard-contact-edition/">Deep League Waiver Wire: Hard Hitting Edition</a><span class="m_author"> by <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=7474">Rylan Edwards</a></span></td></tr><tr>

                    <td>3/25/2016</td><td class="td-badge"><div class="rg badge">RG</div></td><td><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/preston-tucker-cant-hit-from-the-dugout/">Preston Tucker Can't Hit From the Dugout</a><span class="m_author"> by <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=34468">Blake Murphy</a></span></td></tr><tr>
                    <td>8/5/2015</td><td class="td-badge"><div class="rg badge">RG</div></td><td><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/bad-body-preston-tucker/">“Bad Body” Preston Tucker</a><span class="m_author"> by <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=96061">Steven Shumansky</a></span></td></tr><tr>
                    <td>10/10/2014</td><td class="td-badge"><div class="fg badge">FG</div></td><td><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/evaluating-the-prospects-houston-astros/">Evaluating the Prospects: Houston Astros</a><span class="m_author"> by <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/index.php?author=40797">Kiley McDaniel</a></span></td></tr></table></div></td></tr>
            
            </table>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 302px; height: 250px; vertical-align: top;">
            <div class="catchall300" style='width:300px; overflow:hidden;float:right;'><!-- RoS_300x250 --> <div id ='div-gpt-ad-1349421924281-13' style='width:300px; height:250px; overflow:hidden;'><script type='text/javascript'>if ($('#div-gpt-ad-1349421924281-13').is(':visible')) {googletag.cmd.push(function () { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1349421924281-13'); });}</script></div></div>

        </td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        <tr id="so8" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>I've long been optimistic about Tucker's potential, as outlined in <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/get-to-know-preston-tucker/">this Rotographs post</a> from August 2014. Last year, Tucker got an extended look in the majors, displaying a strong power bat with 32 extra-base hits in 323 plate appearances. On the flip side of the coin, he struggled to get on base and received almost zero playing time against lefties. With the Astros picking up Colby Rasmus' one-year, $15 million qualifying offer, it's not easy to find a spot on the Opening Day roster for Tucker. With Rasmus projected to play left field against righties, I don't see a way for Tucker to get regular playing time in the outfield without an injury. It wouldn't surprise me to see Tucker get some work in at first base during Spring Training and/or in Triple-A, where I expect him to start 2016. He's not a good outfielder, and his best route to major-league playing time this season might be at first, where Jon Singleton will likely have an extremely short leash. Tucker has never played a professional inning at first, though he did play the position (rather poorly) for three years in college. (Scott Strandberg)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>With no clear path to playing time, Tucker can be safely ignored in most formats. However, he's someone worth keeping an eye on as the 2016 season gets underway. If things break his way, he does have the tools to make an impact.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
        <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Tucker enjoyed an outstanding four-year college career at the University of Florida and he breezed through the minor leagues fairly easily, as well. Settling into the majors, though, has proved to be more of a challenge. Now 26, Tucker is trying to pick up the pieces after a sophomore season that saw him appear in only 48 games - 50 fewer than during his debut season in ’15. He hit just .164 as his strikeout rate ballooned to 28% despite being a league-average hitter in his freshman campaign. As a bat-first player — with little defensive value — whose best positions are left and right fields, Tucker is in a tough place. He’s proven himself with the bat at every conceivable level except the majors but needs at-bats to prove that he belongs. And that’s not likely to happen in 2017 with the depth that the organization has compiled with veterans such as Josh Reddick, Nori Aoki, and Carlos Beltran - and holdovers such as Evan Gattis and Yulieski Gurriel. The traffic jam gets even more complicated if you consider that unproven players such as Tyler White and A.J. Reed are also looking for playing time at first base and designated hitter (two other possible positions for Tucker). With things being so crowded at the inn, a trade or two may benefit Tucker. Even if he does find a role on the Astros 25-man roster in 2017, though, he’ll likely be in a platoon position given that his career big league OPS is almost .300 points lower against southpaws than right-handers. (Marc Hulet)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Tucker appeared ready to settle into the Astros big league roster after a respectable rookie campaign in 2015 but his sophomore campaign was an absolute disaster. With increased veteran depth on the club, Tucker appears ticketed back to the minors. He shouldn’t be forgotten about entirely but 2017 does not look like his year to be an impact fantasy contributor.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
    </tr>
</table>
